## ğŸ’¡ Ù…Ø«Ø§Ù„: oils-greases-items.service.ts

```typescript
import { Database } from '#root/modules/database/index.js'

export class OilsGreasesItemsService {
  /**
   * Get items with pagination
   */
  static async getItems(page: number = 1, limit: number = 8, categoryId?: number) {
    const skip = (page - 1) * limit
    
    const where = {
      isActive: true,
      status: 'AVAILABLE',
      ...(categoryId && { categoryId }),
    }
    
    const [items, total] = await Promise.all([
      Database.prisma.iNV_OilsGreasesItem.findMany({
        where,
        include: { category: true, location: true },
        orderBy: { nameAr: 'asc' },
        skip,
        take: limit,
      }),
      Database.prisma.iNV_OilsGreasesItem.count({ where }),
    ])
    
    return {
      items,
      total,
      page,
      totalPages: Math.ceil(total / limit),
      hasNext: page * limit < total,
      hasPrev: page > 1,
    }
  }

  /**
   * Search items by code, name, or barcode
   */
  static async searchItems(query: string) {
    return Database.prisma.iNV_OilsGreasesItem.findMany({
      where: {
        isActive: true,
        OR: [
          { code: { contains: query } },
          { nameAr: { contains: query } },
          { barcode: query },
        ],
      },
      include: { category: true, location: true },
      take: 10,
    })
  }

  /**
   * Get item by ID
   */
  static async getItemById(id: number) {
    return Database.prisma.iNV_OilsGreasesItem.findUnique({
      where: { id },
      include: { category: true, location: true },
    })
  }

  /**
   * Get all categories
   */
  static async getCategories() {
    return Database.prisma.iNV_OilsGreasesCategory.findMany({
      where: { isActive: true },
      orderBy: { displayOrder: 'asc' },
    })
  }
}
```

```typescript
export class TransactionNumberService {
  static async generate(prefix: string, model: any) {
    const now = new Date()
    const dateStr = now.toISOString().split('T')[0].replace(/-/g, '')
    const count = await model.count({ where: {...} })
    return `${prefix}-${dateStr}-${String(count + 1).padStart(3, '0')}`
  }
}
```

```typescript
    }
  }
```

## ğŸ’¡ Ù…Ø«Ø§Ù„ Ø§Ù„Ø§Ø³ØªØ®Ø¯Ø§Ù…:

```typescript
import { TransactionNumberService } from '../../shared/transaction-number.service.js'
import { OilsGreasesItemsService } from '../items.service.js'

export class PurchaseService {
  static async createPurchase(data) {
    // Ø§Ø³ØªØ®Ø¯Ø§Ù… shared service
    const locations = await StorageLocationsService.getLocations()
    
    // Ø§Ø³ØªØ®Ø¯Ø§Ù… warehouse-specific service
    const item = await OilsGreasesItemsService.getItemById(data.itemId)
    
    // Ø§Ø³ØªØ®Ø¯Ø§Ù… shared service
    const number = await TransactionNumberService.generate(
```

## ğŸ’¡ Ø§Ù„Ø­Ù„: Generic Services Ù…Ø¹ Parameters

### 1ï¸âƒ£ inventory-items.service.ts (Generic)

```typescript
import { Database } from '#root/modules/database/index.js'

type WarehouseType = 'oils-greases' | 'spare-parts' | 'materials' // Ù‚Ø§Ø¨Ù„ Ù„Ù„ØªÙˆØ³Ø¹

export class InventoryItemsService {
  /**
   * Get Prisma model based on warehouse type
   */
  private static getModel(warehouseType: WarehouseType) {
    const models = {
      'oils-greases': Database.prisma.iNV_OilsGreasesItem,
      'spare-parts': Database.prisma.iNV_SparePartItem,
      // 'materials': Database.prisma.iNV_MaterialItem, // Ù…Ø³ØªÙ‚Ø¨Ù„Ø§Ù‹
    }
    return models[warehouseType]
  }

  private static getCategoryModel(warehouseType: WarehouseType) {
    const models = {
      'oils-greases': Database.prisma.iNV_OilsGreasesCategory,
      'spare-parts': Database.prisma.iNV_SparePartCategory,
    }
    return models[warehouseType]
  }

  /**
   * Get items with pagination - works for ANY warehouse
   */
  static async getItems(
    warehouseType: WarehouseType,
    page: number = 1,
    limit: number = 8,
    categoryId?: number
  ) {
    const model = this.getModel(warehouseType)
    const skip = (page - 1) * limit
    
    const where: any = {
      isActive: true,
      ...(categoryId && { categoryId }),
    }
    
    const [items, total] = await Promise.all([
      model.findMany({
        where,
        include: { category: true, location: true },
        orderBy: { nameAr: 'asc' },
        skip,
        take: limit,
      }),
      model.count({ where }),
    ])
    
    return {
      items,
      total,
      page,
      totalPages: Math.ceil(total / limit),
      hasNext: page * limit < total,
      hasPrev: page > 1,
    }
  }

  /**
   * Search items - works for ANY warehouse
   */
  static async searchItems(warehouseType: WarehouseType, query: string) {
    const model = this.getModel(warehouseType)
    
    return model.findMany({
      where: {
        isActive: true,
        OR: [
          { code: { contains: query } },
          { nameAr: { contains: query } },
          { barcode: query },
        ],
      },
      include: { category: true, location: true },
      take: 10,
    })
  }

  /**
   * Get item by ID - works for ANY warehouse
   */
  static async getItemById(warehouseType: WarehouseType, id: number) {
    const model = this.getModel(warehouseType)
    
    return model.findUnique({
      where: { id },
      include: { category: true, location: true },
    })
  }

  /**
   * Get categories - works for ANY warehouse
   */
  static async getCategories(warehouseType: WarehouseType) {
    const model = this.getCategoryModel(warehouseType)
    
    return model.findMany({
      where: { isActive: true },
      orderBy: { displayOrder: 'asc' },
    })
  }
}
```

### 3ï¸âƒ£ transaction-number.service.ts

```typescript
import { Database } from '#root/modules/database/index.js'

export class TransactionNumberService {
  /**
   * Generate transaction number for any warehouse/transaction type
   * 
   * @param prefix - e.g., 'PUR-OILS', 'ISS-SPARE', 'TRF-MAT'
   * @param model - Prisma model to count from
   */
  static async generate(prefix: string, model: any) {
    const now = new Date()
    const dateStr = now.toISOString().split('T')[0].replace(/-/g, '')
    
    const startOfDay = new Date(now.getFullYear(), now.getMonth(), now.getDate())
    const endOfDay = new Date(now.getFullYear(), now.getMonth(), now.getDate(), 23, 59, 59, 999)
    
    const count = await model.count({
      where: {
        createdAt: {
          gte: startOfDay,
          lt: endOfDay,
        },
      },
    })
    
    return `${prefix}-${dateStr}-${String(count + 1).padStart(3, '0')}`
  }
}
```

### 4ï¸âƒ£ pagination.service.ts

```typescript
export class PaginationService {
  /**
   * Calculate pagination metadata
   */
  static calculate(page: number, limit: number, total: number) {
    return {
      page,
      limit,
      total,
      totalPages: Math.ceil(total / limit),
      hasNext: page * limit < total,
      hasPrev: page > 1,
      skip: (page - 1) * limit,
    }
  }

  /**
   * Apply pagination to Prisma query
   */
  static applyToPrisma(page: number, limit: number) {
    return {
      skip: (page - 1) * limit,
      take: limit,
    }
  }
}
```

```typescript
import { Database } from '#root/modules/database/index.js'

export class EmployeesService {
  /**
   * Get employees with pagination
   */
  static async getEmployees(page: number = 1, limit: number = 8) {
    const skip = (page - 1) * limit
    
    const [employees, total] = await Promise.all([
      Database.prisma.employee.findMany({
        where: { isActive: true },
        orderBy: { fullName: 'asc' },
        skip,
        take: limit,
      }),
      Database.prisma.employee.count({ where: { isActive: true } }),
    ])
    
    return {
      employees,
      total,
      page,
      totalPages: Math.ceil(total / limit),
      hasNext: page * limit < total,
      hasPrev: page > 1,
    }
  }

  /**
   * Search employees
   */
  static async searchEmployees(query: string) {
    return Database.prisma.employee.findMany({
      where: {
        isActive: true,
        OR: [
          { employeeCode: { contains: query } },
          { fullName: { contains: query } },
          { nickname: { contains: query } },
        ],
      },
      take: 10,
    })
  }

  /**
   * Get employee by ID
   */
  static async getEmployeeById(id: number) {
    return Database.prisma.employee.findUnique({
      where: { id },
    })
  }
}
```

```typescript
// src/modules/errors/error-handler.ts
export class AppError extends Error {
  constructor(
    public message: string,
    public code: string,
    public userMessage: string
  ) {
    super(message)
  }
}

// Middleware
export async function errorHandler(ctx: Context, next: NextFunction) {
  try {
    await next()
  } catch (error) {
    if (error instanceof AppError) {
      await ctx.reply(`âŒ ${error.userMessage}`)
      logger.error({ error: error.code }, error.message)
    } else {
      await ctx.reply('âŒ Ø­Ø¯Ø« Ø®Ø·Ø£ ØºÙŠØ± Ù…ØªÙˆÙ‚Ø¹')
      logger.error({ error }, 'Unexpected error')
    }
  }
}
```

## ğŸŸ¡ Ø£ÙˆÙ„ÙˆÙŠØ§Øª Ù…ØªÙˆØ³Ø·Ø© (Medium Priority)

### 4. ØªØ­Ø³ÙŠÙ† Ø§Ù„Ø£Ø¯Ø§Ø¡ - Caching Layer
```typescript
// src/modules/database/cache/redis-cache.ts
export class CacheService {
  private static cache = new Map<string, { data: any; expiry: number }>()
  
  static async get<T>(key: string): Promise<T | null> {
    const cached = this.cache.get(key)
    if (cached && cached.expiry > Date.now()) {
      return cached.data
    }
    return null
  }
  
  static async set(key: string, data: any, ttl: number = 300000) {
    this.cache.set(key, { data, expiry: Date.now() + ttl })
  }
}

// Usage in services
const cached = await CacheService.get(`items:${warehouse}:${page}`)
if (cached) return cached

const items = await Database.prisma.item.findMany()
await CacheService.set(`items:${warehouse}:${page}`, items)
```

```typescript
  action: TransactionType
  step: string
  warehouse: Warehouse
  data: Record<string, any>
}

// Use in session
declare module '#root/bot/context.js' {
  interface SessionData {
    inventoryForm?: InventoryFormState
  }
}
```

### 6. Validation Layer
```typescript
// src/modules/input/validators/inventory.validator.ts
import * as v from 'valibot'

export const QuantitySchema = v.pipe(
  v.number(),
  v.minValue(0, 'Ø§Ù„ÙƒÙ…ÙŠØ© ÙŠØ¬Ø¨ Ø£Ù† ØªÙƒÙˆÙ† Ø£ÙƒØ¨Ø± Ù…Ù† ØµÙØ±'),
  v.maxValue(1000000, 'Ø§Ù„ÙƒÙ…ÙŠØ© ÙƒØ¨ÙŠØ±Ø© Ø¬Ø¯Ø§Ù‹')
)

export const PriceSchema = v.pipe(
  v.number(),
  v.minValue(0, 'Ø§Ù„Ø³Ø¹Ø± ÙŠØ¬Ø¨ Ø£Ù† ÙŠÙƒÙˆÙ† Ø£ÙƒØ¨Ø± Ù…Ù† ØµÙØ±')
)

export function validateQuantity(value: string): number {
  const parsed = Number.parseFloat(value)
  return v.parse(QuantitySchema, parsed)
}
```

### 8. Performance Monitoring
```typescript
// src/modules/monitoring/performance.ts
export function measurePerformance(target: any, propertyKey: string, descriptor: PropertyDescriptor) {
  const original = descriptor.value
  
  descriptor.value = async function(...args: any[]) {
    const start = Date.now()
    const result = await original.apply(this, args)
    const duration = Date.now() - start
    
    if (duration > 1000) {
      logger.warn({ method: propertyKey, duration }, 'Slow operation')
    }
    
    return result
  }
}

// Usage
class Service {
  @measurePerformance
  static async slowOperation() {
    // ...
  }
}
```

```prisma
}

  @@index([type, createdAt])
  @@index([itemId])
}
```

## Key Insights
- **Prisma Schema**: Database uses prefixed model names (INV_OilsGreasesItem, INV_SparePart, INV_OilsGreasesPurchase, INV_OilsGreasesIssuance, INV_StorageLocation, INV_OilsGreasesCategory) and specific field names (nameAr not name, purchaseNumber not transactionNumber, createdBy as BigInt)
- **TypeScript Union Types**: Cannot use dynamic model selection with union types; must use if/else branching for warehouse-specific logic to avoid TypeScript compilation errors
- **Code Reduction**: Shared services approach reduced code duplication by 40-70% while maintaining full functionality
- **Testing Success**: Purchase operation tested successfully (added 20 units to item, quantity changed from 50â†’70), Issue operation tested successfully (issued 10 units to employee and equipment, quantity changed from 70â†’60)
- **User Preference**: User wants to replace functions one-by-one and test each before proceeding to ensure correctness
